class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Ventures II is a beautiful 3D and motion design project created and shared by <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/ryhawthorne\">Ryan Hawthorne.</a> Expanding off of the original series Ventures II continues to explore light, form, scale and perspective. In this iteration of the series Ryan played with a new set of portals and a bit of game theory to create another set of moody, Lo-fi geometric scenes. Ryan is also excited to see where this series goes next as the Ventures continue. href=\"https://www.behance.net/colorsponge\">ColorSponge</a> is a 3D artist with more than 15 years of  experience in the digital world. As many other 3D specialists his first steps were as a self-taught person in the architectural infography, working for small studios in Malaga, Spain as he obtained a university degree in Advertising Design. After many years engaged in the architectural 3D visualization he put all his creativity in diverse fields such as photography, design and composition together to make hyper realistic images for advertising projects. Carlos shares incredible 3D concept cars like this one that I am sharing with you today titled The Brawler. It’s simply awesome, a mix of sports car and batmobile, I would say it. </p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>0310—22\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"http://www.tbpmx.com/\">The branding people</a> shared a branding and visual identity project for Homie, a Mexican online platform that helps millennials land their ideal home by offering users a simplified and intuitive experience. The platform supports the user's journey from the search through to the signing, omitting the typical bureaucracy of renting or buying a new home. </p>\n\n<p>For this rebranding, tbpmx created a concept that revolves around the perfect match between landowners and tenants. The new brand focuses on a playful yet straightforward approach, showcasing a warm color palette alongside a mischievous typography curatorship and inspiring, relatable illustrations that forge a connection between the brand and the users. </p>\n\n<p>Overall, the creation of an affable yet digital graphic system makes finding a new home as easy and flawless as swiping and matching on a dating app. Homie's progressive vision is portrayed through their new brand creating a unique statement within the industry. </p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>Tener un hogar nunca fue tan fácil.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img alt=\"animation  apartment digital home iconography identity ILLUSTRATION  lifestyle room Stationery\"
